We are weekly regulars and the owners memorize our orders. Highly recommend breakfast sandwiches and espresso drinks. They offer a great variety of sweet and savory bagels. <user_id>111761691418843560310</user_id><Rating>4< /Rating><Gmap_id>0x80c2b8dfae6bd759:0x8b43f52c52c57161</Gmap_id>< review>
While searching for a nail salon in Los Angeles that did dip manicures and soak off, I found Powder Nails. It had a great Yelp review and I was able to make an appointment very easily. There's not many nail salons in LA that are open on Monday, so I thought this was a score! It's located at a busy area on La Brea. Street parking is available. I was greeted right away by Sunny, I was already happy because I love that name. She was such a doll! She explained the salon and that her daughter owned it. It's about a year young. There was only one woman doing manicures and one woman doing pedicures, so the whole process was pretty slow. I'm not sure if there's any more staff during the rest of the week, but I was certainly there for a long time. It took me over an hour just to soak off my dip because they didn't use the drill at first. I was able to get my pedicure while my dip was soaking off. I was very happy with my pedicure, but not happy about how long the manicure was taking. Luckily, I was in no rush and I really enjoyed Sunny's sweet disposition and company. At least she always told me how long she thought everything would take. There were a few ladies that came in with broken nails to get fixed, I was hoping that was a coincidence and not that the dip didn't last long for them. I came in and showed Kelly, my manicurist a photo of a natural, french ombre. She said no problem, she would be able to do that. I also had a broken nail that she had to cut off and put on a tip. Shout out to Kimmy who did a great pedicure, Kelly who did a great manicure, and Sunny who did my soak off & who was great all around. My nails, unfortunately only lasted about a week and a half, when they usually last about 2 1/2 weeks, they only looked very good for the first week and the entire experience was very expensive. I loved the decor and Sunny told me that her daughter decorated it. Shout out to the daughter/owner for some seriously amazing decorating skills. I likely won't return here because my nails didn't last long and it was very expensive, but I did enjoy my experience there. I didn't see anyone getting a facial. I noticed they changed their name from Powder Nails & Facial to now Powder Beauty. It was comfortable, laid-back, and they do serve delicious tea!< /review>

It is a nice shopping area, located at Indian Hill Boulevard, at the entrance of City of Claremont. I have been to this area, to shop and look around! There are several stores, including the main grocery store of Super King Markets. Without stores, there are several eateries, located specifically in this area. < Review>
Lots of variety of places to eat in this plaza. From Chinese to Mexican to pizza or sandwiches, there is something for everyone here. The convince of the Super King in this plaza makes this ideal for lunch because you can always go in and grab what you might need for dinner. Parking here however, is a nightmare. You are most likely to find a spot farther away from the entrance of Super King.<//Review>
